		x = 1
		y = 1

		}

			OR = {

		}

			has_government = radical_socialist
			is_puppet = yes
		}

			focus = ENG_Reinforce_Chairman
		}

			factor = 50
		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: ENG_Undermine_Chairman"
			custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_ERC_Increased

				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_ERC_Influence_Low
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ENG_ERC_Influence_Low

				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_ERC_Influence_Medium
